**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Domain Lineage: Envoy xDS Configuration Discovery Service Flow

## Your Task

Trace how an xDS configuration update flows from the control plane to Envoy's data plane. Find: 1. In `envoyproxy/go-control-plane`: the Go source files that define the `DiscoveryRequest` and `DiscoveryResponse` types and the `StreamAggregatedResources` gRPC handler. 2. In `envoyproxy/data-plane-api`: the `.proto` files that define the `AggregatedDiscoveryService` and `DeltaDiscoveryService` RPCs. 3. In `envoyproxy/envoy`: the C++ source files under `source/common/config/` that implement the xDS client subscription logic (look for `GrpcSubscriptionImpl` or `XdsResourceDelegate`). Report the repo, file path, and key type/service name for each hop in the configuration delivery chain.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

## Key Findings

### **1. Control Plane (go-control-plane)**

**Proto Definitions (data-plane-api):**

**Server Implementation:**
- `pkg/server/v3/server.go::StreamAggregatedResources()` (line 189) - Main gRPC handler
- `envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.pb.go` - Generated Go types for `DiscoveryRequest` (line 210) and `DiscoveryResponse` (line 345)
- `envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads_grpc.pb.go` - Generated gRPC service definitions

### **2. Data Plane (Envoy)**

**Subscription Layer:**
- `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h` - `GrpcSubscriptionImpl` class (line 20) adapts typed subscriptions to untyped gRPC mux
- `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.cc::start()` (line 32) - Initiates subscription via `addWatch()`

**Mux Interface:**
- `envoy/config/grpc_mux.h` - Abstract `GrpcMux` interface defining core operations
- Concrete implementations in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h` manage bidirectional streams

### **Configuration Flow Chain**
1. `GrpcSubscriptionImpl::start()` → calls `grpc_mux_->addWatch()`
2. gRPC mux establishes stream via `StreamAggregatedResources` RPC
3. Envoy sends `DiscoveryRequest` with type_url and resource names
4. Control plane's `StreamAggregatedResources` handler receives

When set, Envoy is able to\\n130:   //   terminate if it detects that configuration is stuck at canary. Consider\\n131:   //   this example sequence of updates:\\n132:   //\\n133:   //   * Management server applies a canary config successfully.\\n134:   //   * Management server rolls back to a production config.\\n135:   //   * Envoy rejects the new production config.\\n136:   //\\n137:   //   Since there is no sensible way to continue receiving configuration\\n138:   //   updates, Envoy will then terminate and apply production config from a\\n139:   //   clean slate.\\n140:   //\\n141:   // * ``--dry-run-canary``. Instead, DeltaDiscoveryResponses are a\\n176: // diff to the state of a xDS client.\\n177: // In Delta XDS there are per-resource versions, which allow tracking state at\\n178: // the resource granularity.\\n179: // An xDS Delta session is always in the context of a gRPC bidirectional\\n180: // stream. This allows the xDS server to keep track of the state of xDS clients\\n181: // connected to it.\\n182: //\\n183: // In Delta xDS the nonce field is required and used to pair\\n184: // ``DeltaDiscoveryResponse`` to a ``DeltaDiscoveryRequest`` ACK or NACK.\\n185: // Optionally, a response message level ``system_version_info`` is present for\\n186: // debugging purposes only.\\n187: //\\n188: // ``DeltaDiscoveryRequest`` plays two independent roles. Any ``DeltaDiscoveryRequest``\\n189: // can be either or both of:\\n190: //\\n191: // * Informing the server of what resources the client has gained/lost interest in\\n192: //   (using ``resource_names_subscribe`` and ``resource_names_unsubscribe``), or\\n193: // * (N)ACKing an earlier resource update from the server (using ``response_nonce``,\\n194: //   with presence of ``error_detail`` making it a NACK).\\n195: //\\n196: // Additionally, the first message (for a given ``type_url``) of a reconnected gRPC stream\\n197: // has a third role: informing the server of the resources (and their versions)\\n198: // that the client already possesses, using the ``initial_resource_versions`` field.\\n199: //\\n200: // As with state-of-the-world, when multiple resource types are multiplexed (ADS),\\n201: // all requests/acknowledgments/updates are logically walled off by ``type_url``:\\n202: // a Cluster ACK exists in a completely separate world from a prior Route NACK.\\n203: // In particular, ``initial_resource_versions`` being sent at the \\\"start\\\" of every\\n204: // gRPC stream actually entails a message for each ``type_url``, each with its own\\n205: // ``initial_resource_versions``.\\n206: // [#next-free-field: 10]\\n207: message DeltaDiscoveryRequest {\\n208:   option (udpa.annotations.versioning).previous_message_type = \\\"envoy.api.v2.DeltaDiscoveryRequest\\\";\\n209: \\n210:   // The node making the request.\\n211:   config.core.v3.Node node = 1;\\n212: \\n213:   // Type of the resource that is being requested, e.g.\\n214:   // ``type.googleapis.com/envoy.api.v2.ClusterLoadAssignment``. [#not-implemented-hide:]\\n257:   // Alternative to ``resource_names_unsubscribe`` field that allows specifying dynamic parameters\\n258:   // along with each resource name.\\n259:   //\\n260:   // .. repeated ResourceLocator resource_locators_unsubscribe = 9;\\n265: \\n266:   // Informs the server of the versions of the resources the xDS client knows of, to enable the\\n267:   // client to Flow\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe xDS configuration discovery flow is a bidirectional gRPC streaming mechanism where Envoy (data plane) client subscribes to configuration resources from a control plane server. The flow involves three main components:\\n\\n### 1. Control Plane Server (go-control-plane)\\n\\n**Proto Definitions (data-plane-api):**\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367:envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto` defines the `AggregatedDiscoveryService` with two main RPCs:\\n  - `rpc StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryRequest) returns (stream DiscoveryResponse)`\\n  - `rpc DeltaAggregatedResources(stream DeltaDiscoveryRequest) returns (stream DeltaDiscoveryResponse)`\\n\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367:envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto` defines the core message types:\\n  - `DiscoveryRequest`: Contains `version_info`, `node`, `resource_names`, `type_url`, `response_nonce`, and `error_detail`\\n  - `DiscoveryResponse`: Contains `version_info`, `resources` (list of google.protobuf.Any), `type_url`, `nonce`, and `control_plane`\\n  - `DeltaDiscoveryRequest` and `DeltaDiscoveryResponse` for incremental updates\\n\\n**Server Implementation (go-control-plane):**\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6:pkg/server/v3/server.go::StreamAggregatedResources` (line 189) is the main gRPC handler that receives incoming discovery requests and sends responses\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6:envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads_grpc.pb.go` contains the generated gRPC service definitions for `AggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer` and `AggregatedDiscoveryServiceClient`\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6:envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.pb.go` contains the generated Go structs for `DiscoveryRequest` (line 210) and `DiscoveryResponse` (line 345)\\n\\n### 2. `start()`: Initiates stream with management server\\n  - `addWatch()`: Starts a configuration subscription for specific resources\\n  - `onDiscoveryResponse()`: Handles received discovery responses\\n- The concrete implementations in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h` and `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h` manage the actual bidirectional stream using the gRPC async client\\n\\n**Base Templates:**\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2:source/common/config/subscription_base.h` provides a template-based subscription callback implementation\\n\\n### Configuration Update Flow\\n\\n1. **Subscription Initiation**: Envoy's `GrpcSubscriptionImpl::start()` calls `grpc_mux_->addWatch()` registering interest in resources of a specific type_url (e.g., type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster)\\n\\n2. **Request Transmission**: The gRPC mux establishes a bidirectional stream to the control plane using the `StreamAggregatedResources` RPC and sends the initial `DiscoveryRequest` containing:\\n   - `type_url`: The resource type being requested\\n   - `resource_names`: List of specific resource names (empty means request all resources)\\n   - `node`: Node information identifying the Envoy instance\\n   - `version_info`: Version of last accepted configuration\\n\\n3. **Request Reception**: Control plane's `StreamAggregatedResources` handler receives the `DiscoveryRequest` and queries its configuration cache for matching resources\\n\\n4. **Response Generation**: Control plane sends `DiscoveryResponse` containing:\\n   - `resources`: List of google.protobuf.Any messages containing typed resource configurations\\n   - `type_url`: Matching the request type_url\\n   - `version_info`: New version of this resource set\\n   - `nonce`: Unique identifier for this response\\n\\n5. **Response Processing**: Envoy's GrpcMux receives the response through `onDiscoveryResponse()`, decodes the resources using the registered OpaqueResourceDecoder, and calls the subscription callbacks with the decoded resources\\n\\n6. **ACK/NACK**: Envoy sends back a `DiscoveryRequest` with the same nonce and updated `version_info` to ACK the update, or includes `error_detail` to NACK\\n\\n7. **Delta Updates**: For incremental updates, the Delta RPC (`DeltaAggregatedResources`) uses `DeltaDiscoveryRequest` with `resource_names_subscribe`/`resource_names_unsubscribe` and `DeltaDiscoveryResponse` with only changed/removed resources\\n\\n### Key Type URLs\\n\\nCommon resource types that flow through this system:\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.listener.v3.Listener` (LDS)\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster` (CDS)\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.route.v3.RouteConfiguration` (RDS)\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.endpoint.v3.ClusterLoadAssignment` (EDS)\\n\\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) allows multiplexing all these resource types on a single bidirectional stream, identified by the `type_url` field in each request/response.\"\n}\n",

`start()`: Initiates stream with management server\\n  - `addWatch()`: Starts a configuration subscription for specific resources\\n  - `onDiscoveryResponse()`: Handles received discovery responses\\n- The concrete implementations in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h` and `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h` manage the actual bidirectional stream using the gRPC async client\\n\\n**Base Templates:**\\n- `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2:source/common/config/subscription_base.h` provides a template-based subscription callback implementation\\n\\n### Configuration Update Flow\\n\\n1. **Subscription Initiation**: Envoy's `GrpcSubscriptionImpl::start()` calls `grpc_mux_->addWatch()` registering interest in resources of a specific type_url (e.g., type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster)\\n\\n2. **Request Transmission**: The gRPC mux establishes a bidirectional stream to the control plane using the `StreamAggregatedResources` RPC and sends the initial `DiscoveryRequest` containing:\\n   - `type_url`: The resource type being requested\\n   - `resource_names`: List of specific resource names (empty means request all resources)\\n   - `node`: Node information identifying the Envoy instance\\n   - `version_info`: Version of last accepted configuration\\n\\n3. **Request Reception**: Control plane's `StreamAggregatedResources` handler receives the `DiscoveryRequest` and queries its configuration cache for matching resources\\n\\n4. **Response Generation**: Control plane sends `DiscoveryResponse` containing:\\n   - `resources`: List of google.protobuf.Any messages containing typed resource configurations\\n   - `type_url`: Matching the request type_url\\n   - `version_info`: New version of this resource set\\n   - `nonce`: Unique identifier for this response\\n\\n5. **Response Processing**: Envoy's GrpcMux receives the response through `onDiscoveryResponse()`, decodes the resources using the registered OpaqueResourceDecoder, and calls the subscription callbacks with the decoded resources\\n\\n6. **ACK/NACK**: Envoy sends back a `DiscoveryRequest` with the same nonce and updated `version_info` to ACK the update, or includes `error_detail` to NACK\\n\\n7. **Delta Updates**: For incremental updates, the Delta RPC (`DeltaAggregatedResources`) uses `DeltaDiscoveryRequest` with `resource_names_subscribe`/`resource_names_unsubscribe` and `DeltaDiscoveryResponse` with only changed/removed resources\\n\\n### Key Type URLs\\n\\nCommon resource types that flow through this system:\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.listener.v3.Listener` (LDS)\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster` (CDS)\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.route.v3.RouteConfiguration` (RDS)\\n- `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.endpoint.v3.ClusterLoadAssignment` (EDS)\\n\\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) allows multiplexing all these resource types on a single bidirectional stream, identified by the `type_url` field in each request/response.\"\n}\n",
